        jQuery( document ).ready(function(){

            

            if(jQuery(".ipr_ga_mixed_gallery_page_flag").length > 0)
                ga('ipr.set', 'contentGroup2', 'mixed_gallery');

            ga('ipr.send', 'pageview');

                jQuery(".mixed_gallery_low_res_download, .mixed_gallery_hi_res_download").click(function(){
                    ga_event('mixed_gallery_download',jQuery(this).attr('title'),jQuery(this).attr('data-ipr-ga'));
                    
                       ga_four_event('mixed_gallery_download',jQuery(this).attr('title'),jQuery(this).attr('data-ipr-ga'));
                    
                });

            catch(e){

            }

            try {
                jQuery(".ga-fileview").click(function(){
                  page_id = "67bf85d73d633281c6875f57";
                  user_id = "";
                  if(user_id == ""){user_id='ANONYMOUS'}
                  track_event_label = page_id+"_"+user_id;
                  ga_event('fileView',jQuery(this).attr('data-ipr-ga'),track_event_label);
                  
                     ga_four_event('fileView',jQuery(this).attr('data-ipr-ga'),track_event_label);
                  
                });
            }
            catch(e){

            }


           
            try {
                jQuery('a').click(function(){
                    if(jQuery(this).attr("href") != '' || jQuery(this).attr("href").startsWith("#")){

                        var href = jQuery(this).attr("href")

                        var ismatched = false

                        var social_action = "notset"

                        ga_event('linkClick',jQuery(this).attr("href"),jQuery(this).text());
                        
                           ga_four_event('linkClick',jQuery(this).attr("href"),jQuery(this).text());
                        

                        for (const pattern of social_patterns) {
                            if(href.includes(pattern)) {
                              ismatched = true
                              if(pattern.includes("facebook")){
                                social_action = "facebook";
                              }
                              else if(pattern.includes("twitter")){
                                social_action = "twitter";
                              }
                              else if(pattern.includes("linkedin")){
                                social_action = "linkedin";
                              }
                              else if(pattern.includes("pinterest")){
                                social_action = "pinterest";
                              }
                              else if(pattern.includes("mailto")){
                                social_action = "email";
                              }
                              break;
                            }
                        }

                        if(ismatched){
                            
                               ga_four_event('social',social_action,'https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-announces-financial-results-for-fourth-quarter-and-fiscal-2025');
                            
                        }

                    }

                });
            }
            catch(e){

            }
        });

         var audio_view = function(file_id){
              page_id = "67bf85d73d633281c6875f57";

        var file_view = function(file_id){
              page_id = "67bf85d73d633281c6875f57";
              user_id = "";
              if(user_id == "")
              {
                
                   user_id='ANONYMOUS'

              }

              
         var video_view = function(file_id){
              page_id = "67bf85d73d633281c6875f57";

              track_event_label = page_id+"_"+user_id;

        $(window).on("load", function() {

              if($('video').length){
                 $('video').each(function(){
                    if( $(this).attr('data-fileid') != undefined || $(this).attr('data-fileid') != '')
                    { 
                     file_view($(this).attr('data-fileid'))
                    }
                    else if($(this).closest('.cb-video'))
                    { 
                     if($(this).closest('.cb-video').dataset.filesourceid != undefined)
                     {file_view($(this).closest('.cb-video').dataset.filesourceid)}    
                    }
                 });
              }

              if($('iframe').length){
                $('iframe').each(function(){
                    if($(this).contents().find('video').length){
                        if( $(this).contents().find('video').attr('data-fileid') != undefined || $(this).contents().find('video').attr('data-fileid') != '')
                        { 
                         file_view($(this).contents().find('video').attr('data-fileid'))
                        }
                    }
                });
              }

        });

          </div>
	      </div>

    <div class="main-content col-lg-8">
      <div class="article">
      

        <h1 class="article-title">NVIDIA Announces Financial Results for Fourth Quarter and Fiscal 2025</h1>
        
        <div class="article-subtitle"><ul>
	<li>Record quarterly revenue of $39.3 billion, up 12% from Q3 and up 78% from a year ago</li>
	<li>Record quarterly Data Center revenue of $35.6 billion, up 16% from Q3 and up 93% from a year ago</li>
	<li>Record full-year revenue of $130.5 billion, up 114%</li>
</ul>
</div>
        
        <div class="article-date">
          February 26, 2025
        </div>
        
        <figure class="article-hero">
          <a href="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cms.ipressroom.com/219/files/202502/aabe86db-ce89-4434-b83c-495082979801" download>
            <img
              src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cms.ipressroom.com/219/files/202502/67bf85d33d633281c6875f53_aabe86db-ce89-4434-b83c-49508297980/aabe86db-ce89-4434-b83c-49508297980_mid.jpg"
              alt="NVIDIA Announces Financial Results for Fourth Quarter and Fiscal 2025"
              title="NVIDIA Announces Financial Results for Fourth Quarter and Fiscal 2025"
            />
          </a>
          
        </figure>
        
        <div class="article-body">
         <p>NVIDIA (NASDAQ: NVDA) today reported revenue for the fourth quarter ended January 26, 2025, of $39.3 billion, up 12% from the previous quarter and up 78% from a year ago.</p>

<p>For the quarter, GAAP earnings per diluted share was $0.89, up 14% from the previous quarter and up 82% from a year ago. Non-GAAP earnings per diluted share was $0.89, up 10% from the previous quarter and up 71% from a year ago.</p>

<p>For fiscal 2025, revenue was $130.5 billion, up 114% from a year ago. GAAP earnings per diluted share was $2.94, up 147% from a year ago. Non-GAAP earnings per diluted share was $2.99, up 130% from a year ago.</p>

<p>&ldquo;Demand for Blackwell is amazing as reasoning AI adds another scaling law &mdash; increasing compute for training makes models smarter and increasing compute for long thinking makes the answer smarter,&rdquo; said Jensen Huang, founder and CEO of NVIDIA.</p>

<p>&ldquo;We&rsquo;ve successfully ramped up the massive-scale production of Blackwell AI supercomputers, achieving billions of dollars in sales in its first quarter. AI is advancing at light speed as agentic AI and physical AI set the stage for the next wave of AI to revolutionize the largest industries.&rdquo;</p>

<p>NVIDIA will pay its next quarterly cash dividend of $0.01 per share on April 2, 2025, to all shareholders of record on March 12, 2025.</p>

<p align="justify"><strong>Q4 Fiscal 2025 Summary</strong></p>

<table style="border-collapse: collapse; width:100%; border-collapse:collapse ;">
	<tbody>
		<tr>
			<td colspan="6" style="border-bottom: solid black 1pt ; text-align: center ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; "><strong>GAAP</strong></td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="max-width:40%; width:40%; min-width:40%;;border-top: solid black 1pt ; vertical-align: middle ; "><em>($ in millions, except earnings </em><br />
			<em>per share)</em></td>
			<td style="max-width:12%; width:12%; min-width:12%;;border-top: solid black 1pt ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; "><strong>Q4 FY25</strong></td>
			<td style="max-width:12%; width:12%; min-width:12%;;border-top: solid black 1pt ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; "><strong>Q3 FY25</strong></td>
			<td style="max-width:12%; width:12%; min-width:12%;;border-top: solid black 1pt ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; "><strong>Q4 FY24</strong></td>
			<td style="max-width:12%; width:12%; min-width:12%;;border-top: solid black 1pt ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; "><strong>Q/Q</strong></td>
			<td style="max-width:12%; width:12%; min-width:12%;;border-top: solid black 1pt ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; "><strong>Y/Y</strong></td>
		</tr>

			<td style="vertical-align: middle ; ">Revenue</td>

			<td style="padding-left: 0 ; padding-right: 0 ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">$22,103</td>
			<td style="text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">Up 12%</td>

			<td style="text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">Down 1.6 pts</td>
			<td style="text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">Down 3.0 pts</td>

			<td style="padding-left: 0 ; padding-right: 0 ; text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">$0.78</td>

			<td style="text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">Up 14%</td>
			<td style="text-align: right ;  vertical-align: middle; vertical-align: middle ; ">Up 82%</td>

			<td style="max-width:35%; min-width:35%;;vertical-align: middle ; ">Revenue</td>

<p><strong>Outlook</strong><br />
NVIDIA&rsquo;s outlook for the first quarter of fiscal 2026 is as follows:</p>

<ul type="disc">
	<li>Revenue is expected to be $43.0 billion, plus or minus 2%.</li>
	<li>GAAP and non-GAAP gross margins are expected to be 70.6% and 71.0%, respectively, plus or minus 50 basis points.</li>
	<li>GAAP and non-GAAP operating expenses are expected to be approximately $5.2 billion and $3.6 billion, respectively.</li>
	<li>GAAP and non-GAAP other income and expense are expected to be an income of approximately $400 million, excluding gains and losses from non-marketable and publicly-held equity securities.</li>
	<li style="margin-bottom:8pt;">GAAP and non-GAAP tax rates are expected to be 17.0%, plus or minus 1%, excluding any discrete items.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Highlights </strong></p>

<p>NVIDIA achieved progress since its previous earnings announcement in these areas:&nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Data Center </strong></p>

<ul type="disc">
	<li>Fourth-quarter revenue was a record $35.6 billion, up 16% from the previous quarter and up 93% from a year ago. Full-year revenue rose 142% to a record $115.2 billion.</li>
	<li>Announced that NVIDIA will serve as a key technology partner for the $500 billion Stargate Project.</li>
	<li>Revealed that cloud service providers AWS, CoreWeave, Google Cloud Platform (GCP), Microsoft Azure and Oracle Cloud Infrastructure (OCI) are bringing NVIDIA&reg; GB200 systems to cloud regions around the world to meet surging customer demand for AI.</li>
	<li>Partnered with AWS to make the <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/aws-reinvent-ai-robotics-quantum-software/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA DGX™ Cloud">NVIDIA DGX&trade; Cloud</a> AI computing platform and <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/nim-microservices-aws-inference/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA NIM™ microservices">NVIDIA NIM&trade; microservices</a> available through AWS Marketplace.</li>
	<li>Revealed that Cisco will integrate NVIDIA Spectrum-X&trade; into its networking portfolio to help enterprises build AI infrastructure.</li>
	<li>Revealed that more than 75% of the systems on the <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/top500-supercomputers-sc24/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="TOP500 list">TOP500 list</a> of the world&rsquo;s most powerful supercomputers are powered by NVIDIA technologies.</li>
	<li>Announced a collaboration with Verizon to integrate NVIDIA AI Enterprise, NIM and accelerated computing with Verizon&rsquo;s private 5G network to power a range of edge enterprise AI applications and services.</li>
	<li>Unveiled partnerships with industry leaders including <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-partners-with-industry-leaders-to-advance-genomics-drug-discovery-and-healthcare" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="IQVIA, Illumina, Mayo Clinic and Arc Institute">IQVIA, Illumina, Mayo Clinic and Arc Institute</a> to advance genomics, drug discovery and healthcare.</li>
	<li>Launched <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/agentic-ai-blueprints/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA AI Blueprints">NVIDIA AI Blueprints</a> and <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/nemotron-model-families/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Llama Nemotron model families">Llama Nemotron model families</a> for building AI agents and released <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/nemo-guardrails-nim-microservices/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA NIM microservices">NVIDIA NIM microservices</a> to safeguard applications for agentic AI.</li>
	<li>Announced the opening of NVIDIA&rsquo;s first <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-to-open-vietnam-r-d-center-to-bolster-ai-development" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="R&amp;D center in Vietnam">R&amp;D center in Vietnam</a>.</li>
	<li>Revealed that Siemens Healthineers has adopted <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/rsna-siemens-healthineers-monai-medical-imaging-ai/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="MONAI Deploy">MONAI Deploy</a> for medical imaging AI.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Gaming and AI PC</strong></p>

<ul type="disc">
	<li>Fourth-quarter Gaming revenue was $2.5 billion, down 22% from the previous quarter and down 11% from a year ago.&nbsp;Full-year revenue rose 9% to $11.4 billion.</li>
	<li>Announced new <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-blackwell-geforce-rtx-50-series-opens-new-world-of-ai-computer-graphics" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="GeForce RTX™ 50 Series graphics cards and laptops">GeForce RTX&trade; 50 Series graphics cards and laptops</a> powered by the NVIDIA Blackwell architecture, delivering breakthroughs in AI-driven rendering to gamers, creators and developers.</li>
	<li>Launched GeForce RTX 5090 and 5080 graphics cards, delivering up to a 2x performance improvement over the prior generation.</li>
	<li>Introduced <a href="https://www.nvidia.com/en-us/geforce/news/dlss4-multi-frame-generation-ray-tracing-rtx-games/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA DLSS 4">NVIDIA DLSS 4</a> with Multi Frame Generation and image quality enhancements, with 75 games and apps supporting it at launch, and unveiled <a href="https://www.nvidia.com/en-us/geforce/news/reflex-2-even-lower-latency-gameplay-with-frame-warp/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Reflex 2">NVIDIA Reflex 2</a> technology, which can reduce PC latency by up to 75%.</li>
	<li>Unveiled NVIDIA NIM microservices, <a href="https://www.nvidia.com/en-us/ai-data-science/ai-workflows/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="AI Blueprints">AI Blueprints</a> and the <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/nemotron-model-families/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Llama Nemotron">Llama Nemotron</a> family of open models for RTX AI PCs to help developers and enthusiasts build AI agents and creative workflows.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Professional Visualization</strong></p>

<ul type="disc">
	<li>Fourth-quarter revenue was $511 million, up 5% from the previous quarter and up 10% from a year ago. Full-year revenue rose 21% to $1.9 billion.</li>
	<li>Unveiled <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-puts-grace-blackwell-on-every-desk-and-at-every-ai-developers-fingertips" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Project DIGITS">NVIDIA Project DIGITS</a>, a personal AI supercomputer that provides AI researchers, data scientists and students worldwide with access to the power of the NVIDIA Grace&trade; Blackwell platform.</li>
	<li>Announced generative AI models and blueprints that expand <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-expands-omniverse-with-generative-physical-ai" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Omniverse™">NVIDIA Omniverse&trade;</a> integration further into physical AI applications, including robotics, autonomous vehicles and vision AI.</li>
	<li>Introduced <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/media2/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Media2">NVIDIA Media2</a>, an AI-powered initiative transforming content creation, streaming and live media experiences, built on NIM and AI Blueprints.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>Automotive and Robotics</strong></p>

<ul type="disc">
	<li>Fourth-quarter Automotive revenue was $570 million, up 27% from the previous quarter and up 103% from a year ago. Full-year revenue rose 55% to $1.7 billion.</li>
	<li>Announced that Toyota, the world&rsquo;s largest automaker, will build its next-generation vehicles on <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/toyota-aurora-continental-nvidia-drive" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA DRIVE AGX Orin™">NVIDIA DRIVE AGX Orin&trade;</a> running the safety-certified NVIDIA DriveOS operating system.&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
	<li>Partnered with Hyundai Motor Group to create safer, smarter vehicles, supercharge manufacturing and deploy cutting-edge robotics with NVIDIA AI and <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/hyundai-motor-group-ces/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Omniverse">NVIDIA Omniverse</a>.</li>
	<li>Announced that the <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-drive-hyperion-platform-achieves-critical-automotive-safety-and-cybersecurity-milestones-for-av-development" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA DriveOS">NVIDIA DriveOS</a> safe autonomous driving operating system received ASIL-D functional safety certification and launched the <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/drive-ai-lab-ces/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA DRIVE™ AI Systems Inspection Lab">NVIDIA DRIVE&trade; AI Systems Inspection Lab</a>.</li>
	<li>Launched <a href="https://nvidianews.nvidia.com/news/nvidia-launches-cosmos-world-foundation-model-platform-to-accelerate-physical-ai-development" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Cosmos™">NVIDIA Cosmos&trade;</a>, a platform comprising state-of-the-art generative world foundation models, to accelerate physical AI development, with adoption by leading robotics and automotive companies 1X, Agile Robots, Waabi, Uber and others.</li>
	<li>Unveiled the <a href="https://blogs.nvidia.com/blog/jetson-generative-ai-supercomputer/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano™ Super">NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano&trade; Super</a>, which delivers up to a 1.7x gain in generative AI performance.</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>CFO Commentary</strong><br />
Commentary on the quarter by Colette Kress, NVIDIA&rsquo;s executive vice president and chief financial officer, is available at <a href="https://investor.nvidia.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="">https://investor.nvidia.com</a>.</p>

<p><strong>Conference Call and Webcast Information</strong><br />
NVIDIA will conduct a conference call with analysts and investors to discuss its fourth quarter and fiscal 2025 financial results and current financial prospects today at 2 p.m. Pacific time (5 p.m. Eastern time). A live webcast (listen-only mode) of the conference call will be accessible at NVIDIA&rsquo;s investor relations website, <a href="https://investor.nvidia.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="">https://investor.nvidia.com</a>. The webcast will be recorded and available for replay until NVIDIA&rsquo;s conference call to discuss its financial results for its first quarter of fiscal 2026.</p>

<p><strong>Non-GAAP Measures</strong><br />
To supplement NVIDIA&rsquo;s condensed consolidated financial statements presented in accordance with GAAP, the company uses non-GAAP measures of certain components of financial performance. These non-GAAP measures include non-GAAP gross profit, non-GAAP gross margin, non-GAAP operating expenses, non-GAAP operating income, non-GAAP other income (expense), net, non-GAAP net income, non-GAAP net income, or earnings, per diluted share, and free cash flow. For NVIDIA&rsquo;s investors to be better able to compare its current results with those of previous periods, the company has shown a reconciliation of GAAP to non-GAAP financial measures. These reconciliations adjust the related GAAP financial measures to exclude stock-based compensation expense, acquisition-related and other costs, other, gains from non-marketable and publicly-held equity securities, net, interest expense related to amortization of debt discount, and the associated tax impact of these items where applicable. Free cash flow is calculated as GAAP net cash provided by operating activities less both purchases related to property and equipment and intangible assets and principal payments on property and equipment and intangible assets. NVIDIA believes the presentation of its non-GAAP financial measures enhances the user&rsquo;s overall understanding of the company&rsquo;s historical financial performance. The presentation of the company&rsquo;s non-GAAP financial measures is not meant to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the company&rsquo;s financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, and the company&rsquo;s non-GAAP measures may be different from non-GAAP measures used by other companies.</p>

<a href="https://www.nvidia.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA">NVIDIA</a>&nbsp;(NASDAQ: NVDA) is the world leader in accelerated computing.</p>

Important factors that could cause actual results to differ materially include: global economic and political conditions; NVIDIA&rsquo;s reliance on third parties to manufacture, assemble, package and test NVIDIA&rsquo;s products; the impact of technological development and competition; development of new products and technologies or enhancements to NVIDIA&rsquo;s existing product and technologies; market acceptance of NVIDIA&rsquo;s products or NVIDIA&rsquo;s partners&rsquo; products; design, manufacturing or software defects; changes in consumer preferences or demands; changes in industry standards and interfaces; unexpected loss of performance of NVIDIA&rsquo;s products or technologies when integrated into systems; and changes in applicable laws and regulations, as well as other factors detailed from time to time in the most recent reports NVIDIA files with the Securities and Exchange Commission, or SEC, including, but not limited to, its annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q. Copies of reports filed with the SEC are posted on the company&rsquo;s website and are available from NVIDIA without charge.           <p><strong>About NVIDIA</strong><br />
<a href="https://www.nvidia.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="NVIDIA">NVIDIA</a>&nbsp;(NASDAQ: NVDA) is the world leader in accelerated computing.</p>

<p><br />

Important factors that could cause actual results to differ materially include: global economic and political conditions; NVIDIA&rsquo;s reliance on third parties to manufacture, assemble, package and test NVIDIA&rsquo;s products; the impact of technological development and competition; development of new products and technologies or enhancements to NVIDIA&rsquo;s existing product and technologies; market acceptance of NVIDIA&rsquo;s products or NVIDIA&rsquo;s partners&rsquo; products; design, manufacturing or software defects; changes in consumer preferences or demands; changes in industry standards and interfaces; unexpected loss of performance of NVIDIA&rsquo;s products or technologies when integrated into systems; and changes in applicable laws and regulations, as well as other factors detailed from time to time in the most recent reports NVIDIA files with the Securities and Exchange Commission, or SEC, including, but not limited to, its annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q. Copies of reports filed with the SEC are posted on the company&rsquo;s website and are available from NVIDIA without charge.
